3a1(1): dang thams cad las// brtson 'grus ma rungs ngam du gzung / rdo rje lcags kyu mnga' mgu dang // rin chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan 'dzum// pad+ma ral gri 'khor lo gsung // las dang go
3a2(1): cha 'jigs byed bcangs// thog ma tha ma med cing zhi// ma rungs khro bar bzod pa che// gnod sbyin srin po dam pa brtan// gzi chen dpa' bo dbang po che// u ma'i bdag po skye dgu'i mgon// gtogs 'dod
3a3(1): rgyal 'dod thub pa che// 'jig rten skyong dang mkha' dngas// 'jig rten gsum dang khams gsum pa// 'byung chen sems can don rab mdzad// thams cad gra lang tshangs pa dang // 'khor dang mya ngan 'da'
3a4(1): dang rtag/ yang dag 'tsho dang mchod pa che// sangs rgyas ngag pa theg pa che// srid gsum rtag pa'ang de yin no// 'jig rten gsum rgyal bde skyong dang // bde spyong mgon po rab 'dul mdzad
3a5(1): rdo rje gtsa dang sa rab ma// me shes pa rol phyin pa'i tshul// byang chub sems dpa' rnam par thar// spyod dang de bzhin gshegs pa kun// sangs rgyas don dang sangs rgyas thugs// byang chub kun dang
3a6(1): bla na med// rnam par snang mdzad rgyal dang mgon// rang byung gzungs dang dran pa dang // sems dpa' che dang phyag rgya che// ting 'dzin sangs rgyas 'phrin las mdzad// yang dag sangs rgyas kun bdag nyid/ 
3a7(1): sems can tagadon rtogs mdzad pa// sdong po chen po nag po che// 'dod chags chen po bde ba che// thabs chen dang ni mchog chen mchog/ kun gyi mchog dang gnas dbang po// bcom ldan 'das byang chub chen
3a8(1): ba jigs// byang chub sams dpa' chen po kun tu bzang pon// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ba thugs pa gnasas// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mas cad kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di// dper na gyim
3b1(1): kyi gang bu bzhin du yongs su gang bar gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'dus te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen don thams par grub pa zhes bya ba byang chub kyi sems sing por bzhugs
3b2(1): ba gang na ba der gshegs te/ byang chub sems dpa' de la ched du longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sgra bstan nas/ 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis gang gi phyir// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
3b3(1): cad kyi de kho na nyid mngon par ma rtogs par dka' ba sbyang ba thams cad la spro ba skyed cing / ji ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par bya snyam/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems
3b4(1): dpa' chen po don thams cad grub pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bskul bas mi g.yo ba'i ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag byas nas 'di skad ces gsol to// 
3b5(1): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams de kho na nyid ni ji lta bu lags/ ji ltar ni bsgrub par bgyi ba bka' stsal du gsol// de skad ces gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsung
3b6(1): cig tu 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu rang gi sems la so sor rtogs shing mnyam par zhog la/ rang bzhin gyi grub pa'i sngags 'di ji dgar bzlas shing bsgrub par gyis shig/ oM tsi pA ti bi dI ka rom
3b7(1): de nas byang chub sems dpa' don thams cad grub pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams bdag gi snying po na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lta bur
3b8(1): gda' ba bdag gis rtogs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu sems 'di ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal bas na/ 'di ni ji ltar sbyangs pa de lta bur 'gyur te/ dper na ras
4a1(1): dkar po tshon gyis bsgyur ba bzhin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i sems shes pa brgyas par bya ba'i phyir/ ma~M bo d+hi tsi
4a2(1): ang+ga ta yA mi/ zhes bya ba rang bzhin gyis grub pa'i sngags 'dis yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de byang chub kyi sems bskyed par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpas yang de bzhin
4a3(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi bkas byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas 'di skad ces gsol to// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lta bur mthong ba gang lags pa de ni zla ba'i dkyil 'khor nyid du mthong ngo // de bzhir gshegs
4a4(1): pathams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po sems bskyed pa kun tu bzang po khyod kyis mngon sum du gyur gyis// de legs par sgrubs shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa
4a5(1): thams cad kyi sems bskyed pa kun tu bzang po de brtan par bya ba'i phyir/ sngags 'dis rang gi snying ka'i zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la rdo rje dbyibs su soms shig/ oM tiSh+Tha badz+ra/ byang chub sems
4a6(1): dpas gsol ba/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng mardor bdag gis mthong ngo // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gnyen
4a7(1): ma du pabang po'i gams gas sa pan par tshus shi/ mi ba // des mamam 'i byang thams cad dumam par 'ag pa'o bzhin gshegs pa
4a8(1): klung gamang dgrags nga mji sring pa dang sams cad dab midagags pamasas kyi byin gyi 'arnabs kyis sems dpa rjo da nanas so// de nas ngan zhin gagags pa
4b1(1): cad kyis bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po don thams cad grub pa de la rdo rje'i dbyings/ rdo rje'i dbyings zhes bya ba'i rdo rje mang gi dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje dbying
4b2(1): kyis de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sgran bdag legs par mthong ngo // 
4b3(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ sems dpa' chen po de lta bas na sems dpa' rdo rje de rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi skur bdag nyid rang bzhin gyis
4b4(1): grub pa'i sngags 'di cing gar zlos la sgoms shig/ oM ya thA sarba ta thA ga ta swathA a haM// de nas de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje dbyings kyis bdaganyid de bzhin gshes
4b5(1): par mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag byas te bos nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bdag byin gyis
4b6(1): rlobapa la mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa de bdun par mdzod cig/ de nas de skad ces gsol ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams cad de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dbyings kyi sems dpa' rdo rjer
4b7(1): zhugs sa so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dbyings kyis skad cig ma de nyid kyi tshe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes mngon par rdzogs par
4b8(1): sangs rgyas so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya gsang ba'i dmatshig tu zhugs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos mnyam pa nyid kyi ye na
6a1(1): ting dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyi brlabs kyis cig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi tshad dang mnyam par 'jug pa'i 'od
6a2(1): gzer gyi 'phreng ba can rtse mo lnga pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i rirang bzhin gyi rdo rje ridabyings su gyur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs ka nas byung ste/ 
6a3(1): phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje de las rdo rje la bu'i 'od gzer gzugs dang kha dog sna tshogs pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sdang bas khyab par byed pa rnams byung ngo // rdo rje lta bu'i 'od gzer
6a4(1): de ga ga tsa mo las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rjem yin du phram sring kying bzhin mi shegs pa rnams kyi sgra blang ba/ chos kyi dbyings can du khyab pathams ca dadang rnamama'agi khams kyi mapar gtugs
6a5(1): thams cad dang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab 'byam rgya mtsho'i sprinathams cadang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes mngon par shes pa mngon par byang chub pas/ 
6a6(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub kyi sems chen po bskyed pa dang / kun tu bzang ba'i spyod pa sna tshogs sgrub pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs mnyes par mdzad pa dang / byang chub
6a7(1): stong ba chen por gshegs pa dang / bdud thams cad gdul ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi byang chub chen por mngon par byang chub pa dang / ngam chos kyi 'khor lo bskor
6a8(1): banas/ ngi srid sems can gyi khams ma las shing lus pa med pa rnams yongs sa slob cing thams cad la phan pa dang / zad bar mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ma shes dang
6b1(1): mngon bar shes pa dam pa'i dngos grub sgrub pa la sogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul rnams bar du brtan nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni kun tu bzang
6b2(1): po nyid yin pa dang / shin tu brtan pa nyid yin pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i skur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs
6b3(1): sa gnas nas/ cheng du brjod pa 'di cheng du brjod do// e ma'o bdag ni rang 'byung ba'i// kun tu bzang po'i sems dpa' brtan// de ni bstan phyir lus min yang // sems dpa'i lus sa gyur
6b4(1): ba yin/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i sku bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs panas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyan sngan zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lo gnas nas bka'
6b5(1): nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa
6b6(1): thams cad kyi tshul khrims dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / shes rab dang / rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / sems can gyi don bya ba
6b7(1): dang / thabs chen po dang / stobs dang / brtson 'grus dang / ye shes chen po'i dam tshig sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa yongs su bskyab pa dang / thams cad kyi dbang po
6b8(1): bya ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de srid de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes dang mngon par shes pa bla na med pa'i theg pa chen po
7a1(1): mngon par rtogs pa'i grub pa'i mchog thob pa'i bar du/ 'bras bu de dag gi phyir byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po de/ de bzhin gshegs pa
7a2(1): thams cad kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku rin po che ni pang bu rgyan dang cod pan gyi dbang gyi dbang gis dbang bskur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi grub
7a3(1): pa dzi rjong de'i lag par byed no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis lag na rdo rje lagan rdo chags rdo ming gi dbang gis dbang 'thar ro// ngas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa
7a4(1): chen po phyag na rdo rje phyag g.yon pa rdo rje bsgyings par bzhugs/ phyag g.yas pas rdo rje thugs kar gsor zhing 'phen pa'i tshul du 'dzin cing ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun
7a5(1): gyis grub pa yi// rdo rje bla na med pa 'di// bdag ste bdag gi lag tu byin// rdo rje la ni rdo rje gnas// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gdon mam
7a6(1): pa'i rgyal po'i dam tshig las byung ba'i sems dpa' byin gyis brlabs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba
7a7(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra dang/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs ka nas blang ma thag du 'dzin/ bcom ldan 'das byan
7a8(1): marje nying de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi lcags kyu chen por gyur te byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas// rdo rje zhugs
7b1(1): than pa'i tshangs sa gyur te/ bamathan 'das kyi phyag gnyis suganas so// denas rdu zugs bur bubs chen pa delas 'jig rten gyi 'am sa thams cad kyi rdul shin du pa ma nga mnam pa'
7b2(1): bzhin gshegs pa'i surnams byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cang spyan drang ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin
7b3(1): ni shin tu gdon mi za bar rgyal ba nyid yin pa dang / shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po gdon mi za ba'i rgyal po'i lus su gyur nas/ bcom ldan
7b4(1): 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o rdo rje las byung ba'i// lcags kyu nges pa'i rgyal po bdag/ gang phyir kun tu sangs rgyas khyab/ 
7b5(1): grub phyir kun nas spyan 'dren no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po shin tu gdon mi za ba'i rgyal po'i sgra bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
7b6(1): g.yas phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan 'dren pa'i ngamacho
7b7(1): gardo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan 'dren pa'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad
7b8(1): dgug pa dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'dra ba'i byin gyis brlabs dam pa'i dngos grub kyi bar gyi phyir/ rdo rje lcags kyu
8a1(1): byang chub sems dpa'i gdon mi za ba'i rgyal po de'i lag par de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje 'grags pa rdo rje 'gregs pa zhes bya bar
8a2(1): dbang gi dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje 'gugs pa rdo rje'i lcags kyu des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan 'dren cing che dang brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas
8a3(1): dran gyi dzi si e gres blan me pa'adi/ sangs rgyas par gyi grub byor// sanas spyan 'dren dam pa'o// de nas mang bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po bdud ces bya ba'i dam tshigams
8a4(1): byung ba'i sems pa'i byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams
8a5(1): cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra rA ga/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de// de bzhin gshegs pa
8a6(1): mas cad kyi mi tog gi mang gra nas byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad tsagrags su zhugs te// gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje mang 'chen po'i dbyibasas gyur te/ b+hag gangs susam
8a7(1): so/ de nas rdorje'i mda' byibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu tha mong nga mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgran mas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rjes sum nyes pa
8a8(1): bya ba la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin shin du bdud byed pa dang / rab tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sem
8b1(1): ba can po bdud ces bya ba gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mngang kyi zugs la gsus mdzang ched du brjod pa'ang chang du brjod do// e ma'o bdag gi ring bzhin dag/ rang 'byung ba dgang gyes byeng ma/ 
8b2(1): 'dod chags bra rnams dag pa'i phyir/ 'dod chags kyis ni 'dul bar byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po bdang de'i lus bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs gnas byung ste/ nga bzhin gshegs pa mas
8b3(1): cad kyi g.yon phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang ka' nod cing bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par bya ba'i byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i
8b4(1): ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdung rdo rje'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams mgu bar bya ba dang / thams cad kyi
8b5(1): bde ba dang / yid bde ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdud kyi las kyi dngos grub kyi mchog thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir rdo rje'i mnga' de byang chub sems dpa' chen po bdud ces bya ba de'i lag tu
8b6(1): de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bdud byed cing / ched du brjod pa'ang ched du brjod do// kyis rdo rje rigazhu zhes bya ba'i dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa'
8b7(1): sems dpa' chen po rdo'i gzhu zhes bya bas/ rdo rje'i mngab des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bdud byed cing / ched du brjod pa 'di cheng du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi 'dod chags kyi// ye shes 'di
8b8(1): ni dri ma med// 'dod chags kyi ni chags bral bcom// bde ba thams cad sbyin par byed// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yang byang chub sems dpa' chen po rab tu dga' ba'i rgyal po'i dam tshig las byung ba'i
9a1(1): sems dpa'i byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rab tu dga' ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba de bzhin
9a2(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra sA d+ha/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de legs
9a3(1): so zhes bya ba'i gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje dgyes pa'i dbyibs su gyur te/ phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje dgyes pa'i
9a4(1): dbyings de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi legs so// zhes bya ba la sogs
9a5(1): pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams byas nas rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu dga' bar byed pa dang / rab tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ 
9a6(1): byang chub sems dpa' rab tu dga' ba'i rgyal po'i lus su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o thams
9a7(1): cang mkhyen kun gyi// legs byin nang na bdag mchog pas// rnam rtog bral ba de dag gi/ nges par dgyes pa bskyed pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rab tu dga' ba'i rgyal po'i rtsa
9a8(1): de bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyab na/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bka'i dod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom
9b1(1): ldan 'angasu bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i rdorje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rab tu dgyes pa bla na med dang ma shes pa
9b2(1): dmatshig sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i sems can thams cad mgu bar bya ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang ying bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de nas pazhin gshegs pa
9b3(1): thams cad dgyes pa'i ro bla na med pa dam pa 'grub pa thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir rdo rje dgyes pa de byang chub sems dpa' chen po rab tu dga' ba'i rgyal po nga'i lag tu de bzhin du byin mo
9b4(1): denas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje dgyes pa rdo rje dgyes pa zhes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dbang gis bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje dgyes pas
9b5(1): rdo rje dgyes pa'i dbyibs nges de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la legs so zhes bya bas rab tu dgyes par byed cing ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi legs byin pa/ 'di ni rab tu 'jug
9b6(1): byed pas// rdo rje thams cad dgyes par byed pa'i lha rdzas dgyes pa spel ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba'i dmatshig dang / 
9b7(1): de nas bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i ye shes dang / dgyes pa chen po dang / 'di bzhin ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig chen po'i sems dpa'o// de nas yang
9b8(1): bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i dam tshig las byung ba rin po che'i byin gyi brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs
10a1(1): pa thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badrarat+na/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams
10a2(1): nga gyi thugs lam byung mjam thag pa 'dzin rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin thams cad nam mkha' dang mnyam par nyid kyi ye shes shin tu rtogs pa yin pa'i phyir ro// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de nas
10a3(1): mkha' thams cad kyi 'od gzer du gyur nas byung ngo // nam mkha' thams cad kyi 'od gzer de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byas pas thams cad nam mkha'i dbyings lta bur gyur to// 
10a4(1): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis nam mkha'i dbyings de dag thams cad bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin shin du bsgom
10a5(1): par gyur pa'i phyir/ yang nam mkha'i khams thams cad las byung ba 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mnyam par 'jug pa'i tshad tsam rdo rje rin po che chen po'i dbyings su gyur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag
10a6(1): gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje rin po che'i dbyings de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sgrar gyur nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
10a7(1): cang byengad bang la sogs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'dral rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi snying po las shin
10a8(1): tra byung ba dang / rab tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i spang po'i sbrang gur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mad kyi thugs la gnas nas/ ched du brjod pa 'ding che
10b1(1): drabarjod do// sem tshogs med rgyal ba yang/ khams gsum dbang por dgongs param/ dza chen ngam pa mi/ dbang mi mchog ni bdag min no// de nas byang chubasams dpa' cher po ma mdza da
10b2(1): sras bcom ldan 'das kyis drugs nas blang na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kun tham thaba'i kyil 'khor la gnas nam yang ba' nang kyang bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis debs na/ 
10b3(1): thathams cad kyino bu rin po rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la sgoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa yongs sa rdzogs par bya ba'i ngamatshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma las
10b4(1): shing lus pa med pa'i don thams cad yongs su grub par bya ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dor phun sum tshogs pa'i grub pa thob par
10b5(1): bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i rdo rje rin po che chen po 'khor lo bskor bar/ rdo rje che rin po che myu gu'i dbang gis dbang bskur nas/ lag tu rdo rje'i nor bu de byin no// de nas de
10b6(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje snying po zhes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying pos rdo rje nor bu de rang gi dbang bskur ba'i gnas su 'jog cing ched du brjod pa
10b7(1): 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi sems kyi sems dpa'i dbyings// dbang bskur de ni bdag yin te// bdag gi lag tu byin pas na// rin chen la ni ron chen bzhag/ de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis
10b8(1): byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzi brjid chen po zhes bya ba'i dam tshig las byung ba'i rin po che'i byin gyi brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od bzer
11a1(1): gyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra te dza/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las phyung ma thag
11a2(1): pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen por gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje nyi ma'i dbyings su gyur te/ 
11a3(1): bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams rnams kyi sku byung
11a4(1): nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od gzer 'gyed pa la sogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu gzi brjid che ba nyid
11a5(1): dang / shin du brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzi brjid chen po'i skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ 
11a6(1): ched du brjod pa'ang ched du brjod do// e ma'i sems can khams kun du// snang byed gzi brjing dpe med bdag/ gang phyir sangs rgyas dag pa yi// 'dzin pa rnams kyang sbyong bar byed// de nas
11a7(1): byang chub sems chen po dri ma med pa'i gzi brjid de'i lus bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi g.yas phyogs su zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas te/ 
11a8(1): bka donod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la sgoms par zhugs
11b1(1): nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gzer gyi dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams kyi gzi brjid mtshungs pa med pa dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang ying bded
11b2(1): myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi 'od 'thob cing dngos grub dam pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ rdo rje nyim de byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzi brjid chen po
11b3(1): de'i lag tu de bzhin du byin no// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje 'od rdo rje 'od nyim nges de bzhin
11b4(1): gshegs pa thams cad la snang bar byed cing / ched du brjod pa 'ang ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi snang ba 'di// mi shes mun nag 'joms byed pa// shin tu phra rdul ji snyid pa'i// nyi ma'i 'ong bas nin
11b5(1): tu lhag/ de nas yang bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po rini dpal gyi dam tshig las byung ba rin po che'i byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de nas
11b6(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i dam tshig zhes bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra ke ru/ de nas de bzhin
11b7(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las phyung ma thag pa 'di ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de/ rgyal mtshan kha dog dang gzugs dang rgyan dang dbyibs sna tshogs par gyur te/ byung nas bcom ldan
11b8(1): 'das rnam par sna mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dbyibs su gyur te/ phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi
12a1(1): khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che'i rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba la sogs pa
12a2(1): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rin po che chen po'i dpal dang shin tu brtan pa yin pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa'
12a3(1): chen po rin po che dpal gyi skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o// don kun grub pa dang // dgongs pa thams cad rdzogs
12a4(1): pa yi// don rnams thams cad rdzogs byed pa'i// 'dra med dpal ni bdag yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rin po che'i dpal gyi sku bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs
12a5(1): pathams cad kyi gson gyi phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang bka' don cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan gyi byin gyi rlabs
12a6(1): zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis nor bu ying bzhin gyi rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams kyi'i
12a7(1): thams cad yongs su banang bar bya ba dang thams cad kyi bde dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi don chen po'i dngos grub dam pa thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi byor/ 
12a8(1): rdodza rgyal maman byang chub sems dpa' rten pa rin po che dngal de'i la gadrang bzhin byiran no// nganas de bzhi gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rgyal mtshan rdo rgya mtsham zhes bya ba ni ji rje ming gi bang gi
12b1(1): dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sbyan pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sbyor du bcug nas/ rtserang
12b2(1): brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi dgongs pa kun// yongs su rdzogs par byed pa yi// yid bzhin nor bu rgyal mtshan 'di/ sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin pa'i rgyal// de nas bcom
12b3(1): ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po'i dam tshig las byung ba rin po che'i byin gyi brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ 
12b4(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgyes pa'i dam tshig zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra hA sa/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
12b5(1): kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dzum par gyur te/ byung nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su
12b6(1): zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje 'dzum pa'i dbyibs su gyur te phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje 'dzum pa'i dbyibs de las/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin
12b7(1): du phra ba dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rmad du byung ba la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul
12b8(1): rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rtag tu dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po yin pa dang shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas// byang chub sems dpa' chen po
13a1(1): rtag tu dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po'i lus su gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnams par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ ched du brjod pa 'ang che du brjod do// 
13a2(1): du mjam par gzhag rnams kyi// sangs rgyas don la rab sbyor phyir// e ma'o bdag ni kun mchog gi/ bzhad chen rmang byung chen po yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu mas
13a3(1): ba'i dbang po'i lus bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyab kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// 
13a4(1): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rmang du byung ba'i byin gyi brlabs zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rmad du
13a5(1): byung ba bskyed pa'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad kyi dbang po bla na med pa thams cad bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin
13a6(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang po yongs su spong ba'i ye shes mngon par shes pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po de'i lag tu
13a7(1): rje'adzum pa de de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje dga' ba rdo rje dga' ba zhes rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
13a8(1): bordo rje dga' bas/ rdo rje 'dzum pa des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgyes par byed cing / ched du brjod pa'ang ched du brjod do// 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ rmang du 'byung bskyed sngon
13b1(1): pras kyis chen myong brab lags so// gtsug lag gzhan gyis shes mnus// dbang bskur ba tsho chen pa dang // 'od kyi dkyil 'khor 'angom gang dang / sems dpa' chen pa dzin
13b2(1): dang / dgyes pa chen po dang 'di bzhin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba chen po'i sems dpa'o// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen
13b3(1): kun du spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i dam tshig las byung ba'i chos kyi byin gyi brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos
13b4(1): kyi dam tshig zhes bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas phyung ngo // badz+ra d+harmA/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa
13b5(1): 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rang bzhin gyis dag pa'i chos mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rab tu rtogs pa'i phyir/ dam pa'i chos kyi 'od gzer du gyur
13b6(1): te byung ngo // dam pa'i chos kyi 'od gzer de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du kun tu snang bar byas nas chos kyi rang bzhin du gyur to// chos kyi dbyings de dag thams cad kyang bcom ldan 'das
13b7(1): rnam par snang ma dang rtsi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ nam mkha'o khams thams cadadang mnyam par 'jug pa'i tshang tsam gyis rdo rje pad+ma chen po'i dbyibs su gyur te/ drug 'i
13b8(1): su gnas so// de nas rdo rje pad+ma'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ting
14a1(1): nge 'dzin gyi ye shes dang mngon par shes pa la sogs par dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams 'jig rten gyis khams
14a2(1): thams cad du byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po yin pa dang shin tu brtan pa'i phyir/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ 
14a3(1): byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i skur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas nas/ ched du brjod
14a4(1): pa'ang ched du brjod do// e ma'o rang 'byung gdod nas dag/ dam pa'i don ni bdag yin te// gang phyir gzings 'dra'i chos rnams las// rnam par dag pa dmigs par gyur/ 
14a5(1): de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi lus de bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyan
14a6(1): bA na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas te/ bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi ma ngam pa nyid ye shes
14a7(1): dmatshig las byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par grags nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thamam cang rnam par snang ba'i dmatshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shi
14a8(1): lus pa med pa rnams kyis bdag dang gzhan rnam par dag par bya ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi ye shes
14b1(1): dang mngon par shes pa drug thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun du lhan ras gzigs kyi dbang po ngas pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba nyid dang / dbazhin
14b2(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi sgra'i dbang gis dbang bskur nas/ de'i lag tu rdo rje pad+mo byin no// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje'i rgyan rdo rje'i sbyin nas rdon ming gi dbang gis
14b3(1): dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje spyan gyis rdo rje'i pad+mo'i 'dab ma de la 'byed pa'ing/ 'dod chags rnam par dag cing ma chags pa ngo bo nyid du gzigs pas
14b4(1): gzigs shing ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod// sangs rgyas kun gyi 'dod chags kyis// de yi kho nas rtogs pa 'di// bdag ste bdag gi lag du byin// chos la chos ni gnas par gyur// de nas
14b5(1): yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gyi dam tshig las byung ba'i chos kyi byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin
14b6(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab dang ye shes chen po'i dam tshig ces bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra tik+Sh+Na/ de nas de bzhin gshegs
14b7(1): pathams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de shes rab kyi ye shes kyi ral grir gyur te/ byung nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs
14b8(1): te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje ral gri'i dbyibs su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje ral gri'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin
15a1(1): tum mo dang mjam pa di bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab kyi ye shes la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad
15a2(1): rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams bya ste/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu 'jam pa'i ngagra yin pa dang / shin tu brtan pa yin pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems
15a3(1): dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i skur gyur ste/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad
15a4(1): kyi/ 'jam dbyangs bdag ni yin par dgongs/ gang phyir shes rab gzugs med kyang // dbyangs nyid du ni dmigs pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gyi sku
15a5(1): de bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis g.yas phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur te/ 
15a6(1): denas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab kyi rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa
15a7(1): rnams card gcad pa'i mtshug dang / sems can gyi khams ma lum shing lus pa med pa'i lhag bsnga ma thams cad bcad pa dang / mas ca rgya ba ba dang med pade bsung
15a8(1): thabanas de bdin gagags thathams cad kyi phu rnas su 'bras 'azung b.rigs mngan pa mangs su tshanam par bya 'a' bar du'athas tha dadag ga cing / tham
15b1(1): chub sems dpa' chen po'ajam dpal gyi lag tu de bzhin gan du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i zla zhes bya ba rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro// nganas rgya
15b2(1): chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i blos de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rdo rje'i ral grings 'debs shing // ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// shes na
15b3(1): pha rol phyin pa'i tshul// dgra rnams thams cad gcod byed cing // sdig pa thams cad 'joms pa'i mchog/ de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po sems bskyed
15b4(1): ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor 'di dam tshig las byung ba chos kyi byin brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo'i dam
15b5(1): tshig ces bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sdong po 'di rang gi thugs gnas phyung ngo // badz+ra he du/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni/ bcom ldan
15b6(1): 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po la sogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor du gyur te byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi
15b7(1): thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje 'khor lo'i dbyibs su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gnyis su gnas par gyur to// de nas rdo rje 'khor lo'i dbyibs de las 'jig
15b8(1): rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku rnams byung ste/ sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas
16a1(1): rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi tsho byang rnams 'jig rten gyi khams chung du byas te/ rdo rje sems dpa'i dang nge 'dzin ni sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi bar ma pa nar ba dzin pangs
16a2(1): tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi das mes skor ba zhes bya ba'i skar gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang ma
16a3(1): grags la gnas nas ched dadu brjod pa 'di ched brjod do/ rdo rje dam pa chos can gyi/ oM mdo rdo rje 'a khor lo bdag gang phyir sems bskyed dum gyis kyang // chos kyi khar ma bskor bar gyur/ 
16a4(1): de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor bskor ba'i swA de/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thug tha las byang ste/ de bzhin gzigs pa thams cad kyi g.yo phyogs kyi
16a5(1): ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur na/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhug/ 
16a6(1): nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor chen po'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus zhing lus pa med par 'jug dpyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / thams cad kyi bde bad
16a7(1): yid bde 'amyong bar banas/ de bzhini gshegs pa thams cad kyi ma 'a'i chos kyi 'khar mo bskor ba dam pa 'grub pa'i bar dra'abras brad dag gi phyir/ rdo rje'i 'khor ma byang chub sems dpa
16a8(1): chen po sems bskyed ma thag bcas kyi bar ma bskor ba de'i lag tun bzhin du byin no// rnams branin gzhag d+hab thams cad kyil rdo rje snying za rdo rje seM dziMn rdo rje mang gi dbang gis 'gyur ba/ sa
16b1(1): brang rnabasams dpa' sems dpa' can brda rjeni sring bamarda rje'i 'khar ma das de bzhin gshags pa thams cad rkye mi ldag pa cing du dadzag cang chad du brjod pa'ang chang dra brjod pa 'di ni gangs rgyas
16b2(1): thams cad kyi/ chos rnams thams cad rnam par spyod/ phyir mi ldog la'i 'khor lo ni// byang chub snying po yin par bshad// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po mi gsung
16b3(1): pa'i dam tshig las blang ba/ chos tu byin gyis brlags rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bzlas pa'i dam tshig ces byas par bzhin yan

16b5(1): gshegs pa thams cad chos nyid kyi yi ger gyur te byang nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje bzlas pa'i dbyibs su gyur te phyag bcis
16b6(1): sraganas so// de nas rdo rje'i bzlas pa'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ma dang / mnam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgra rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa
16b7(1): thams cad kyi chos nyid la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdo rje rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul la sogs pa byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu tshig ma yin pa dang / 
16b8(1): shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po tshig ma yin pa'i skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ ched du
17a1(1): brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o rang 'byung rnams kyi gsang // ldem po ngag du bdag dgongs// gang bI dam pa'i chos 'chang ba// tshig tu spros las rnam par bras
17a2(1): de nas byang chub sems dpa' tshig ma yin pa'i skad/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgya ba na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ de bzhin gshegs
17a3(1): thams cad kyi gsu yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i gsung rdo rje'i mtshig las byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting / 
17a4(1): de 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi ye shes kyi dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus zhing lus med pa rnams kyi tshig sgrub pa
17a5(1): dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba med par byas nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi gsang ba nid thob pa'i dngos grub dam pa'i bar gyi phyir/ rdo rje bzlas
17a6(1): pa de byang chub sems dpa' chen po tshig ma yin pa'i lag tu de bzhin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad pa thams cad kyis rdo rje'i tshig rdo rje'i tshig zhes rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dab
17a7(1): bskur ro/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i tshig gis/ de bzhin gzhags pa thams cad la rdo rje'i bzlas pa das mang dag par gyu du rbang du brjod pa'in med du brdan pa/ 'dzin/ 
17a8(1): sangs rgyal thams cad kyi// rdo rje bzlas par brjod pa min// de bzhin gzhags pa thams cad kyi// sngags da myu du 'argya bar 'gyur// rdo rje rje ma nyid kyim nas dang // de na na gnas
17b1(1): ba thams cad kyi shes ran rgya ma zhes dang / rab rgya shes dang / chos kyi 'char mo chen po bskor ba'i ye nas dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung rga ma
17b2(1): pa rnam par ldog pa'i ye shes te/ 'di bzhin ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi sems dpa' chen po'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams
17b3(1): cad kyi byang chub sems dpa' chen po las thams cad pa zhes bya ba'i tshig las byung ba las byin brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs
17b4(1): pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin de gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'dir rang gi thugs ka nas byung ngo do/ de nas rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni las thams

17b6(1): cad kyi 'phrin las kyi 'od gzer du gyur te byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi 'od gzer de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byas nas/ de bzhin gshegs
17b7(1): gas pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dbyibs lta bur gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dbyings ma lus pade yang bcom ldan 'das rnams par snang mdzad kyi thugs
17b8(1): sa rmugs te/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad dang mnyam pa'i tshad tsam du gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dbyings de las/ las kyi rdo rje'i dbyings su gyur nas
18a1(1): phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku rnams byung ste/ 
18a2(1): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i rting

18a4(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las thams cad ces bya ba'i skur gyur te// bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs kar gnas nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched
18a5(1): dra brjod do// e ma'o sangs rgyas rnams kyi des// phrin las mang po kun bdag yin// sangs rgyas don ni lhan grub phyir// rdo rje las ni 'jug par 'gyur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen
18a6(1): bde bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las thams ces bya ba'i lus bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyan sngar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas te yang bka' nad cing
18a7(1): bzhugs par gyur to/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gnags pa jam cad kyi mdzin mo za ba'i dmaklas byung ba rdo rje'i drin zlar gyis derlangs zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par grags nas
18a8(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sa mchod bar bya ba la sogs pa gdon mi zang tshang med pa dang / las kyi chog rgyas pa thams cad kyi mchig dang thams can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa

18b3(1): kyi 'khor lo bskor bar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dbang gis dbang bskur nas/ de'i lag tu las kyi rdo rje de de gshegs pa rnams kyis rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro//

18b8(1): las byung ma thag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de nyid de/ go cha brtan par gyur te/ byung nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par sna mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres pa mthun

19a2(1): drapra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bsrung ba'i cho ga rgyas pa'i las la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'ju

21a2(1): dpa'i zhing nge 'dzin na de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur shin tu bcings pa dang / rab tu 'dres par brtan pa'i phyir/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po de bzhin

21a7(1): can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa mong ba rnams la de bzhin gnags pa thams cad dang / lha rnams kyi dgongs par brtag pa dang / grub thams cad kyis bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/

21b2(1): chen po rdo rje 'a chur zhes bya ba des/ rdo rje bcing ba des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'ching zhing ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ phyag rgya bcings pa che zhing brtan/
